INNER JOIN (
    SELECT a0."Id", a0."ImageURL", a0."Name", a."ActorsId", a."MoviesId"
    FROM "ActorMovie" AS a
    INNER JOIN "Actors" AS a0 ON a."ActorsId" = a0."Id"
) AS t ON m."Id" = t."MoviesId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a1."ActorsId", a1."MoviesId", m0."Id", m0."BannerURL", m0."Description", m0."DirectorId", m0."Duration", m0."Genres", m0."ImageURL", m0."ImdbRating", m0."ImdbRatingCount", m0."Name", m0."OriginalName", m0."ReleaseDate", m0."UserRating", m0."UserRatingCount"
    FROM "ActorMovie" AS a1
    INNER JOIN "Movies" AS m0 ON a1."MoviesId" = m0."Id"
    WHERE m0."Id" = @__get_Item_0
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."ActorsId"
WHERE m."Id" = @__get_Item_0
ORDER BY m."Id", t."ActorsId", t."MoviesId", t."Id", t0."ActorsId", t0."MoviesId"

So typical for the Russian culture spirit of mischief, which is, actually, never punished, and the notion that relative welfare not necessarily means happiness made the book by Astrid Lindgren and its TV adaptations tremendously popular in the Soviet Union and nowadays Russia and vice versa - somewhat alienated to the Western reader and viewer (see User's comments below). SELECT t."Id", t."ImageURL", t."Name", m."Id", t."ActorsId", t."MoviesId", t0."ActorsId", t0."MoviesId", t0."Id", t0."BannerURL", t0."Description", t0."DirectorId", t0."Duration", t0."Genres", t0."ImageURL", t0."ImdbRating", t0."ImdbRatingCount", t0."Name", t0."OriginalName", t0."ReleaseDate", t0."UserRating", t0."UserRatingCount"
FROM "Movies" AS m
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT a0."Id", a0."ImageURL", a0."Name", a."ActorsId", a."MoviesId"
    FROM "ActorMovie" AS a
    INNER JOIN "Actors" AS a0 ON a."ActorsId" = a0."Id"
) AS t ON m."Id" = t."MoviesId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a1."ActorsId", a1."MoviesId", m0."Id", m0."BannerURL", m0."Description", m0."DirectorId", m0."Duration", m0."Genres", m0."ImageURL", m0."ImdbRating", m0."ImdbRatingCount", m0."Name", m0."OriginalName", m0."ReleaseDate", m0."UserRating", m0."UserRatingCount"
    FROM "ActorMovie" AS a1
    INNER JOIN "Movies" AS m0 ON a1."MoviesId" = m0."Id"
    WHERE m0."Id" = @__get_Item_0
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."ActorsId"
WHERE m."Id" = @__get_Item_0
ORDER BY m."Id", t."ActorsId", t."MoviesId", t."Id", t0."ActorsId", t0."MoviesId"
